id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2><font style="color: #000000;"><span class="h1"><font size="2"><strong>Smith &amp; Wesson&nbsp;</strong></font></span> <span class="h1"><font size="2"><strong><span>M&amp;P Shield .40 Smith &amp; Wesson 3.1" Barrel, Black Melonite Finish, Polymer Frame, One 6 Round and One 7 Round Magazine</span></strong></font></span></font></h2> <h3><font style="color: #000000;" face="book antiqua,palatino" size="2"><span>Extremely thin and lightweight design means that it can be comfortably carried all day. Single-sided thumb safety and slide stop maximize slimness. M&amp;P s patented take down lever and sear deactivation system allows for disassembly without pulling the trigger. Includes 2 magazines; 1 with extended capacity for full grip. 18 degree grip angle for natural point of aim. Striker-fired for short and consistent trigger pull every time. White dot front sight, white 2 dot rear sight. Stainless steel barrel and slide with polymer frame. Black Melonite 68 HRc barrel/slide finish.</span></font></h3> <p><font size="2"><span style="font-size: small;">Smith &amp; Wessons new M&amp;P SHIELD is a slim, concealable, lightweight, striker-fired polymer pistol. Available in 9mm and .40 S&amp;W, the new M&amp;P SHIELD features a slim design combined with the proven and trusted features found in the M&amp;P Pistol Series. From the pistols easily concealed one-inch profile to its optimized 18-degree grip angle, the M&amp;P SHIELD offers professional-grade features that provide consumers with simple operation and reliable performance. Chambered in 9mm and .40 S&amp;W for proven stopping power, the M&amp;P SHIELD features a high-strength polymer frame with a black, Melonite coated stainless steel slide and barrel. Both models are standard with a 3.1-inch barrel, which contributes to an overall length of 6.1 inches and an unloaded weight of 19 ounces. For fast tracking and smooth target acquisition, the M&amp;P SHIELD is standard with a 5.3-inch sight radius and has been enhanced with a short, consistent trigger pull measuring 6.5 pounds. Featuring a quick and audible reset made possible by the striker-fired action, the M&amp;P SHIELD allows multiple rounds to be placed on target both consistently and accurately.</span></font></p> <p><font size="2"><span>ALL BACKED BY THE SMITH &amp; WESSON LIFETIME SERVICE POLICY.</span></font></p> <p><span><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/SW/sw_shield_c.jpg" alt="" width="544" height="251"><br></span></p> <p><span><br></span></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Pistols</li><li>Type : Pistol</li><li>Action : Double</li><li>Caliber : 40 Smith &amp;
